[{"bookPath":"","title":"Frontends","titleId":"ref-frontends","hasOtp":true,"hasPageHeader":true},"<h1 id=\"ref-frontends\" class=\"refHeader\">Frontends<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" frontends.<a href=\"#p_0\" class=\"pid\">0</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_1\" class=\"pid\"></i>Frontends are implemented in <a href=\"/frontend/#ref-frontends-js\">JavaScript</a>\n  or via <a href=\"/rpc/js/#ref-frontends-rpc-js\">JavaScript</a>,\n  <a href=\"/rpc/go/#ref-frontends-rpc-go\">Go</a>, and\n  <a href=\"/rpc/py/#ref-frontends-rpc-py\">Python</a>.<a href=\"#p_1\" class=\"pid\">1</a>\n</p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js\" class=\"refHeader\">JavaScript<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-js\"><span class=\"icon var(--shiki-color-text)\">(env);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_3\" class=\"pid\"></i>When you use <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/tool/#cmd_reach%20run\" title=\"cmd: reach run\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">reach run</span></a></span> or <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/tool/#cmd_reach%20react\" title=\"cmd: reach react\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">reach react</span></a></span>, you don't need to do anything else.<a href=\"#p_3\" class=\"pid\">3</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_4\" class=\"pid\"></i>However, most developers when they stop learning and experimenting will use their own testing or deployment infrastructure.\n  At that point, you should install the <a href=\"https://www.npmjs.com/package/@reach-sh/stdlib\" target=\"_blank\"><code>@reach-sh/stdlib</code></a> <a href=\"https://www.npmjs.com/\" target=\"_blank\"><code>npm</code></a> package however you prefer installing packages.\n  For example, you can use <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">npm</span></span>:<a href=\"#p_4\" class=\"pid\">4</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div if you are running your frontend without <code>reach</code> or using a tool like <a href=\"https://webpack.js.org/\" target=\"_blank\">webpack</a> for deployment.<a href=\"#p_5\" class=\"pid\">5</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_6\" class=\"pid\"></i>If you want to install the standard library for a browser application or library and you are using a bundler <strong>without</strong> standard library, you need to remember the JavaScript representation of each of the Reach types:<a href=\"#p_7\" class=\"pid\">7</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_Contract\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"Contract\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"// Reach   => JavaScript\nNull       => var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> value]</span></li><li value=\"17\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Struct     </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> object</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_8\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, the Reach type <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">MInt </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Data\" title=\"rsh: Data\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Data</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({None</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Null</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Some</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> UInt})</span></span> inhabitant <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">MInt</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.Some</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">42</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">)</span></span> is represented as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">[</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'Some'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">42</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">]</span></span> in JavaScript.<a href=\"#p_8\" class=\"pid\">8</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_9\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_Bytes\" title=\"rsh: Bytes\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Bytes</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(len)</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_BytesDyn\" title=\"rsh: BytesDyn\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">BytesDyn</span></a></span> may be represented as either a <code>'string'</code> or a <code>Uint8Array</code> byte array.\n  Both types are accepted as input.\n  If the input string is prefixed with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">0x</span></span>, the string will be interpreted as hex.\n  Reach will output a value as a <code>'string'</code> if the value is able to be encoded in UTF-8.\n  Otherwise, the value will be represented as <code>Uint8Array</code> byte array.<a href=\"#p_9\" class=\"pid\">9</a>\n</p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js-loader\" class=\"refHeader\">Loading the Standard Library<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-js-loader\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h1>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_loadStdlib\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"loadStdlib\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_Reach\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"Reach\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"import { loadStdlib } from '@reach-sh/stdlib';\nconst stdlib = loadStdlib(env);\n\n// or, equivalently\nimport { Reach } from '@reach-sh/stdlib';\nconst stdlib = new Reach(env);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn5\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/import\" title=\"js: import\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">import</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> { loadStdlib } </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">from</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'@reach-sh/stdlib'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/const\" title=\"js: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">loadStdlib</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(env);</span></li><li value=\"3\"></li><li value=\"4\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// or, equivalently</span></li><li value=\"5\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/import\" title=\"js: import\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">import</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> { Reach } </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">from</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'@reach-sh/stdlib'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"6\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/const\" title=\"js: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">new</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_Reach\" title=\"js: Reach\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">Reach</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(env);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_10\" class=\"pid\"></i>Returns the standard library based on the provided <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">env</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_10\" class=\"pid\">10</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_11\" class=\"pid\"></i>You may call this function multiple times and get completely separate standard libraries, with different (and incompatible!) configuration options.<a href=\"#p_11\" class=\"pid\">11</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_12\" class=\"pid\"></i>In environments where the Reach standard library has implicit access to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">process</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.env</span></span>,\n  you may omit the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">env</span></span> argument, in which case <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">process</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.env</span></span> will be used.\n  If the standard library is being used with JavaScript bundlers like Webpack\n  ---as it is with React, for example---\n  then Reach does <strong>not</strong> have implicit access to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">process</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.env</span></span>.\n  In such scenarios, we recommend that you call this function like so:<a href=\"#p_12\" class=\"pid\">12</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const stdlib = loadStdlib(process.env);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn6\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/const\" title=\"js: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_loadStdlib\" title=\"js: loadStdlib\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">loadStdlib</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">process</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.env);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_13\" class=\"pid\"></i>Alternatively, you can construct a custom object that has all of the environment keys and fields you need.\n  Each network supports different keys; see <a href=\"/networks/#ref-networks\">Networks</a> for details.<a href=\"#p_13\" class=\"pid\">13</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_14\" class=\"pid\"></i>As a special case, you may instead pass in the string <code>'ETH'</code> or <code>'ALGO'</code>,\n  to select the desired connector directly.<a href=\"#p_14\" class=\"pid\">14</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_15\" class=\"pid\"></i>By default, this method allows a user to load a standard library for a single connector.\n  That is, this method may not be called multiple times with varying connectors.\n  To bypass this restriction, use <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs\" title=\"js: unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_15\" class=\"pid\">15</a>\n</p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"import { unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs } from '@reach-sh/stdlib';\nunsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs() => null\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn7\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/import\" title=\"js: import\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">import</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> { unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs } </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">from</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'@reach-sh/stdlib'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs\" title=\"js: unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">unsafeAllowMultipleStdlibs</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">() </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">null</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_16\" class=\"pid\"></i>Calling this function will lift the restriction that\n  <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_loadStdlib\" title=\"js: loadStdlib\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">loadStdlib</span></a></span> imposes on loading multiple standard libraries.<a href=\"#p_16\" class=\"pid\">16</a>\n</p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js-provider\" class=\"refHeader\">Provider Selection<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-js-provider\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h1>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_17\" class=\"pid\"></i>The first thing you should do in a frontend is decide if you need to specify a provider.\n  This process works differently in the browser than in console (or \"automated\") contexts.<a href=\"#p_17\" class=\"pid\">17</a>\n</p>\n<h2 id=\"ref-frontends-wallets\" class=\"refHeader\">Providers in Browsers via Wallets<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-wallets\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p><i id=\"p_18\" class=\"pid\"></i>By default, in browsers, Reach will automatically attach to a standards-conforming wallet, which is a connector-specific concept:<a href=\"#p_18\" class=\"pid\">18</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li><i id=\"p_19\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Ethereum, MetaMask is used as the standard.<a href=\"#p_19\" class=\"pid\">19</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_20\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Algorand, <a href=\"https://github.com/algorandfoundation/ARCs/blob/main/ARCs/arc-0011.md\" target=\"_blank\">ARC-0011</a> is used as the standard.<a href=\"#p_20\" class=\"pid\">20</a></li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_21\" class=\"pid\"></i>However, in your user does not have a standards-conforming wallet, then you can set up a fallback for them.<a href=\"#p_21\" class=\"pid\">21</a></p>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_22\" class=\"pid\"></i>As of late 2022, almost no Algorand users have ARC-0011 wallets, so you should almost certainly use this function!<a href=\"#p_22\" class=\"pid\">22</a></p>\n</div>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_stdlib.setWalletFallback\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"stdlib.setWalletFallback\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"stdlib.setWalletFallback(make: () => wallet): void\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn8\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.setWalletFallback\" title=\"js: stdlib.setWalletFallback\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.setWalletFallback</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(make: () </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> wallet): </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_23\" class=\"pid\"></i>When you call this function, if no browser wallet is available, then <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">make</span></span> will be called to construct one and it will be installed as if there were always a browser wallet.<a href=\"#p_23\" class=\"pid\">23</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_24\" class=\"pid\"></i>The value that <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">make</span></span> should conform to the connector-specific standard (mentioned above).<a href=\"#p_24\" class=\"pid\">24</a></p>\n<hr>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_25\" class=\"pid\"></i>Please refer to the <a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/algo-wallet-demo\" target=\"_blank\"><code>algo-wallet-demo</code></a> example to see a full walkthrough of this discussion.<a href=\"#p_25\" class=\"pid\">25</a></p>\n</div>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_26\" class=\"pid\"></i>Since this function installs a new value as the browser wallet, if you call <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.setWalletFallback\" title=\"js: stdlib.setWalletFallback\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.setWalletFallback</span></a></span> twice, then the second is guaranteed to do nothing, <em>even if you are using different standard library instances</em>, because this modifies a global property of the browser.\n  If you want to work around that, then you'd have to delete the property so that Reach cannot find a browser wallet on the second time.<a href=\"#p_26\" class=\"pid\">26</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_27\" class=\"pid\"></i>For example, this is a bad program that is useless:<a href=\"#p_27\" class=\"pid\">27</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"const stdlib1 var(--shiki-token-comment)\">// uses make1's result</span></li></ol></pre>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_stdlib.walletFallback\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"stdlib.walletFallback\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"stdlib.walletFallback(opts: object): () => wallet\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn12\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.walletFallback\" title=\"js: stdlib.walletFallback\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.walletFallback</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(opts: object): () </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> wallet</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_31\" class=\"pid\"></i>This function returns a value that may be passed to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">setWalletFallback</span></span> to synthesize a wallet for use in browsers that do not supply a compliant wallet.\n  Its customization options, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">opts</span></span>, depend on the connector.<a href=\"#p_31\" class=\"pid\">31</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_32\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Ethereum, it always errors and cannot provide a wallet.<a href=\"#p_32\" class=\"pid\">32</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_33\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Algorand, it can provide a wallet that directly connects to the Algorand network, like <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">setProviderByName</span></span> (&amp; <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">setProviderByEnv</span></span>), but provide interactive signing.\n  The network connection is specified via the <code>providerEnv</code> key, which may be a string (which is used as an argument to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">providerEnvByName</span></span>) or an environment (which is used as an argument to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">setProviderByEnv</span></span>).\n  Alternatively, a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">BasicProvider</span></span> value can be provided with the key <code>provider</code> (see <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.setProvider\" title=\"js: stdlib.setProvider\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.setProvider</span></a></span>'s documentation to understand the type of this value).<a href=\"#p_33\" class=\"pid\">33</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_34\" class=\"pid\"></i>By default, signing is via an interactive browser window prompt, where the user repeatedly provides their mnemonic.\n  But, other fallbacks can be synthesized by providing special arguments in <code>opts</code>.<a href=\"#p_34\" class=\"pid\">34</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_35\" class=\"pid\"></i>If the key <code>MyAlgoConnect</code> is provided, and bound to the default export of <code>@randlabs/myalgo-connect</code>, then <a href=\"https://wallet.myalgo.com/home\" target=\"_blank\">MyAlgo</a> will be used for signing.\n  For example, this sets the wallet fallback to be MyAlgo used with Algorand TestNet:<a href=\"#p_35\" class=\"pid\">35</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"import MyAlgoConnect from '@randlabs/myalgo-connect';\nstdlib.setWalletFallback(stdlib.walletFallback({\n  providerEnv: 'TestNet', MyAlgoConnect }));\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn13\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/import\" title=\"js: import\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">import</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> MyAlgoConnect </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">from</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'@randlabs/myalgo-connect'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"2\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.setWalletFallback\" title=\"js: stdlib.setWalletFallback\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.setWalletFallback</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.walletFallback\" title=\"js: stdlib.walletFallback\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.walletFallback</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">({</span></li><li value=\"3\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  providerEnv</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'TestNet'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> MyAlgoConnect }));</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_36\" class=\"pid\"></i>Alternatively, you can call the <code>ALGO_MakeAlgoSignerConnect</code> export <code>@reach-sh/stdlib</code>, with the <code>AlgoSigner</code> global object from <a href=\"https://github.com/PureStake/algosigner\" target=\"_blank\">AlgoSigner</a> and a provider name to use the AlgoSigner extension.\n  For example, this sets the wallet fallback to be AlgoSigner and the Algorand TestNet:<a href=\"#p_36\" class=\"pid\">36</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"import { ALGO_MakeAlgoSignerConnect as MakeAlgoSignerConnect } from '@reach-sh/stdlib';\nstdlib.setWalletFallback(reach.walletFallback({\n  providerEnv, MyAlgoConnect: MakeAlgoSignerConnect(AlgoSigner, 'TestNet') }));\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn14\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/import\" title=\"js: import\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">import</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> { ALGO_MakeAlgoSignerConnect </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">as</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> MakeAlgoSignerConnect } </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">from</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span export of <code>@reach-sh/stdlib</code> on the default exports of <code>@walletconnect/client</code> and <code>algorand-walletconnect-qrcode-modal</code>, then <a href=\"https://walletconnect.com/\" target=\"_blank\">WalletConnect</a> is used to connect to the <a href=\"https://perawallet.app/\" target=\"_blank\">PeraWallet</a> for signing.\n  For example, this sets the wallet fallback to be WalletConnect and the Algorand TestNet:<a href=\"#p_37\" class=\"pid\">37</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" <code>@reach-sh/stdlib</code>, with <code>PeraWalletConnect</code> from <code>@perawallet/connect</code>, then PeraConnect is used to connect to the <a href=\"https://perawallet.app/\" target=\"_blank\">PeraWallet</a> for signing.\n  For example, this sets the wallet fallback to be PeraConnect and the Algorand TestNet:<a href=\"#p_38\" class=\"pid\">38</a>\n</p>\n<pre style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'TestNet'</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> WalletConnect</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: fallback exposes the underlying WalletConnect wrapper object as the <code>wc</code> property on the wallet.\n  Furthermore, it supports using an existing WalletConnect wrapper object by providing the key <code>WalletConnect_wc</code> in the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.walletFallback\" title=\"js: stdlib.walletFallback\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.walletFallback</span></a></span> options object.\n  (When you're using PeraConnect, the same object/keys/etc are used for the <code>PeraWalletConnect</code> object.)<a href=\"#p_39\" class=\"pid\">39</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><i id=\"p_40\" class=\"pid\"></i>Because these are fallbacks, you need to decide for your users which wallet they'll use, or make a user interface element to let them select which wallet fallback to use.<a href=\"#p_40\" class=\"pid\">40</a></p>\n<div class=\"note\">\n  <p><i id=\"p_41\" class=\"pid\"></i>Please refer to the <a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/algo-wallet-demo\" target=\"_blank\"><code>algo-wallet-demo</code></a> example to see a full walkthrough of using wallet fallbacks and all their options.<a href=\"#p_41\" class=\"pid\">41</a></p>\n</div>\n<h2 id=\"ref-frontends-providers-raw\" class=\"refHeader\">Providers not using Wallets<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-providers-raw\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p><i id=\"p_42\" class=\"pid\"></i>If you are not building a browser-based DApp, you may want to set the network provider by using a standard name or using environment variables:<a href=\"#p_42\" class=\"pid\">42</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_stdlib.setProviderByName\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"stdlib.setProviderByName\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"stdlib.setProviderByName(string) => void\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn17\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.setProviderByName\" title=\"js: stdlib.setProviderByName\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.setProviderByName</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(string) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_43\" class=\"pid\"></i>Supported provider names are: <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'MainNet'</span></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'TestNet'</span></span>, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'BetaNet'</span></span>, and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'LocalHost'</span></span>.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'BetaNet'</span></span> is sometimes referred to as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'DevNet'</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_43\" class=\"pid\">43</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_44\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Ethereum, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'MainNet'</span></span> will connect to homestead, and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'TestNet'</span></span> to ropsten.\n  Multiple free API providers are used behind the scenes, <a href=\"https://docs.ethers.io/v5/api/providers/#providers-getDefaultProvider\" target=\"_blank\">as implemented by ethers.js</a>.<a href=\"#p_44\" class=\"pid\">44</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_45\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Algorand, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'MainNet'</span></span> will connect to MainNet, and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'TestNet'</span></span> to TestNet.\n  The default Node provider is AlgoNode, but the free <a href=\"https://randlabs.io/products?product=api\" target=\"_blank\">RandLabs API</a> provider can also be used.<a href=\"#p_45\" class=\"pid\">45</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_46\" class=\"pid\"></i>Provider connections are created with the code below:<a href=\"#p_46\" class=\"pid\">46</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">MainNet</span></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p><i id=\"p_60\" class=\"pid\"></i>There are a few options to customize how Reach interacts with the Provider, however it is found.<a href=\"#p_60\" class=\"pid\">60</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_setMinMillisBetweenRequests\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"setMinMillisBetweenRequests\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_61\" class=\"pid\"></i>Setting this to a positive number forces outgoing requests to occur one at a time,\n  and limits them to occur no more frequently than one request every <code>ms</code> milliseconds.\n  This is only supported with certain connectors,\n  and applies to all Providers created by the Reach standard library.<a href=\"#p_61\" class=\"pid\">61</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_setCustomHttpEventHandler\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"setCustomHttpEventHandler\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" value=\"1\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_setCustomHttpEventHandler\" title=\"js: setCustomHttpEventHandler\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.setCustomHttpEventHandler</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(h: (e</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span id=\"p_62\" class=\"pid\"></i>Allows for the installation of a custom hook to observe outgoing HTTP requests.\n  The handler <code>h</code> will be called before and after every request.\n  The handler will be called with one argument: an object <code>e</code>.\n  Inspection of <code>e</code>'s fields should be considered an unstable API that may change over time.\n  Currently, it has a field <code>eventName</code> which may be <code>'before'</code>, <code>'success'</code>, or <code>'error'</code>,\n  as well as various other fields describing the HTTP event.\n  This is only supported with certain connectors,\n  and applies to all Providers created by the Reach standard library.<a href=\"#p_62\" class=\"pid\">62</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" class=\"pid\"></i>Allows for the installation of a custom hook to observe signing requests.\n  The handler <code>h</code> will be called on every request.\n  The <code>evt</code> argument is an unstable object that describes the request.\n  The <code>pre</code> argument is a Promise of an unstable object with details about the request, available after the request has been made.\n  The <code>post</code> argument is a Promise of an unstable object with details about the completed request, available after the request has been completed.<a href=\"#p_63\" class=\"pid\">63</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_64\" class=\"pid\"></i>Example:<a href=\"#p_64\" class=\"pid\">64</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Promise</span></span> will only be resolved after the transfer completes.<a href=\"#p_120\" class=\"pid\">120</a>\n</p>\n<p><i class=\"pid\">121</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_122\" class=\"pid\"></i>Algorand-only options:<a href=\"#p_122\" class=\"pid\">122</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_123\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">closeTo</span></span> An <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Address</span></span> to which all remaining ALGO will be sent before the sender account is closed.\n    If <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">token</span></span> is specified, the sender account opts out of the token rather than closing.\n    See <a href=\"https://developer.algorand.org/docs/get-details/transactions/#close-an-account\" target=\"_blank\">this page</a> for more information.\n    The default is no close address.<a href=\"#p_123\" class=\"pid\">123</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_124\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">note</span></span> A <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Uint8Array</span></span> for the <code>Note</code> field of the asset creation transaction.\n    The default is a note containing the Reach version used to perform the transfer.<a href=\"#p_124\" class=\"pid\">124</a>\n  </li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_125\" class=\"pid\"></i>Example:<a href=\"#p_125\" class=\"pid\">125</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a {\n  await stdlib.transfer(accAlice, accBob, stdlib.parseCurrency(1));\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn76\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"24\"><span style=\"color: id=\"p_126\" class=\"pid\"></i>This transfers one (1) unit of the network token from Alice's account <code>accAlice</code>, to Bob's account <code>accBob</code>.<a href=\"#p_126\" class=\"pid\">126</a></p>\n<h2 id=\"ref-frontends-js-acc-eth\" class=\"refHeader\">EVM-specific (Ethereum)<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-js-acc-eth\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h2>\n<p><i id=\"p_127\" class=\"pid\"></i>When connected to an EVM-based consensus network, the standard library provides additional functionality.<a href=\"#p_127\" class=\"pid\">127</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_setGasLimit\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"setGasLimit\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"acc.setGasLimit(n) => void\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn77\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">acc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_setGasLimit\" title=\"js: setGasLimit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.setGasLimit</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(n) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_128\" class=\"pid\"></i>Modifies the gas limit for each transaction originating from the given account for the rest of the program.\n  <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">n</span></span> must be a value that <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_bigNumberify\" title=\"js: bigNumberify\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">bigNumberify</span></a></span> will accept.<a href=\"#p_128\" class=\"pid\">128</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_129\" class=\"pid\"></i>On EVM-based consensus networks, the Reach standard library will automatically estimate the required gas necessary to execute transactions, i.e. make publications.\n  However, sometimes this estimation process is inaccurate, especially when Reach programs interact with remote objects.\n  In those cases, it is sometimes useful to specify a particular gas limit.\n  It is common on Ethereum to use gas limits like <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5000000</span></span> in testing.\n  If you do this, you should inform your clients that they should pay attention to the gas stipend issued.<a href=\"#p_129\" class=\"pid\">129</a>\n</p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\"><a href=\"https://github.com/reach-sh/reach-lang/tree/master/examples/atomic-swap/index.mjs\">/examples/atomic-swap/index.mjs</a><a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"  const myGasLimit = 5000000;\n  accAlice.setGasLimit(myGasLimit);\n  accBob.setGasLimit(myGasLimit);\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn78\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"30\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/const\" title=\"js: const\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">const</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">myGasLimit</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5000000</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">;</span></li><li value=\"31\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">accAlice</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_setGasLimit\" title=\"js: setGasLimit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.setGasLimit</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(myGasLimit);</span></li><li value=\"32\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">  </span><span style=\"color: style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(myGasLimit);</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_130\" class=\"pid\"></i>Here, there is a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">myGasLimit</span></span> object created, which is set to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">5000000</span></span>.\n  This is then applied to both the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">accAlice</span></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">accBob</span></span> by using the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_setGasLimit\" title=\"js: setGasLimit\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">setGasLimit</span></a></span> method so that the maximum gas cost is set for each account.<a href=\"#p_130\" class=\"pid\">130</a>\n</p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js-ctc\" class=\"refHeader\">Creating a Contract Handle<a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-js-ctc\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h1>\n<p><i id=\"p_131\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_ctc\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"ctc\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_contract\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"contract\"></span>The third thing you should do in a frontend is create a contract handle, so you can actually interact with your Reach program.<a href=\"#p_131\" class=\"pid\">131</a></p>\n<hr>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"acc.contract(bin: Backend, info?: Promise<ContractInfo>) => Contract\nstdlib.contract(bin: Backend, info?: Promise<ContractInfo>) => Promise<Contract>\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn79\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">acc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_contract\" title=\"js: contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.contract</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(bin: Backend</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> info</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">?:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">) </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Promise</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_Contract\" title=\"js: Contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Contract</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_132\" class=\"pid\"></i>Returns a Reach contract handle based on the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">bin</span></span> argument, and optional <code>ContractInfo</code> provided.\n  The <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">acc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_contract\" title=\"js: contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.contract</span></a></span> form will use the account <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">acc</span></a></span> to interact with the returned contract.\n  The <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_contract\" title=\"js: contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.contract</span></a></span> form is equivalent to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(</span><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Operators/await\" title=\"js: await\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">await</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_createAccount\" title=\"js: createAccount\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.createAccount</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">()).contract</span></span>, generating an account on demand\n  (this means the contract can only be used for read-only operations).\n  This <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">bin</span></span> argument is the module produced by <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/tool/#cmd_reach%20compile\" title=\"cmd: reach compile\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">reach compile</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_132\" class=\"pid\">132</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_133\" class=\"pid\"></i>If <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">info</span></span> is provided, it must be a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ContractInfo</span></span> value, or a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Promise</span></span> that eventually yields a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ContractInfo</span></span> value.\n  When provided, Reach will verify that the contract given actually matches the bytecode produced by <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/tool/#cmd_reach%20compile\" title=\"cmd: reach compile\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">reach compile</span></a></span> and will error if it is different in any way.<a href=\"#p_133\" class=\"pid\">133</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_134\" class=\"pid\"></i>Typically, the deployer of a contract will not provide <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">info</span></span>, while users of a contract will.\n  In an automated, single instance program, <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">ctc</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.getInfo</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">()</span></span> is typically used to acquire <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">info</span></span>;\n  while in non-automated programs, an application uses out-of-band communication, such as an external database or user input, to acquire the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">info</span></span> argument.<a href=\"#p_134\" class=\"pid\">134</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_135\" class=\"pid\"></i>The first publishing participant will attempt to deploy a contract for an application.\n  If <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">info</span></span> was provided, an error will be thrown.\n  This deployment can only happen one time, so subsequent attempts will fail with an error.<a href=\"#p_135\" class=\"pid\">135</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_136\" class=\"pid\"></i>This function may emit warnings if there is any danger, risk, or subtlety to using this contract on your chosen consensus network.\n  You can omit this warning by setting <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">REACH_NO_WARN</span></span>, but we recommend that you do not.<a href=\"#p_136\" class=\"pid\">136</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_137\" class=\"pid\"></i>The <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">acc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_contract\" title=\"js: contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.contract</span></a></span> form of the function does not block.<a href=\"#p_137\" class=\"pid\">137</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_getInfo\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"getInfo\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"ctc.getInfo() => Promise<ContractInfo>\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn80\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_ctc\" title=\"js: ctc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">ctc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_getInfo\" title=\"js: getInfo\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.getInfo</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">() </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Promise</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ContractInfo</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_138\" class=\"pid\"></i>Returns a Promise for a <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ContractInfo</span></span> value that may be given to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_contract\" title=\"js: contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">contract</span></a></span> to construct a Reach contract handle for this contract.\n  This object may be stringified with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">JSON</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">stringify</span></span> for printing and parsed again with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">JSON</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">parse</span></span> without any loss of information.<a href=\"#p_138\" class=\"pid\">138</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_139\" class=\"pid\"></i>If <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_ctc\" title=\"js: ctc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">ctc</span></a></span> will deploy the program, then the Promise will only be resolved after the contract is actually deployed on the network,\n  thus you cannot block on this Promise with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Operators/await\" title=\"js: await\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">await</span></a></span> until after the first <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/step/#rsh_publish\" title=\"rsh: publish\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">publish</span></a></span> has occurred.\n  Awaiting <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">getInfo</span></span> too early may cause your program to enter a state of deadlock.\n  It is safer to make an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/local/#rsh_interact\" title=\"rsh: interact\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">interact</span></a></span> function that receives <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_getContract\" title=\"rsh: getContract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">getContract</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">()</span></span> from the Reach program.<a href=\"#p_139\" class=\"pid\">139</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_getContractAddress\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"getContractAddress\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"ctc.getContractAddress() => Promise<Address>\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn81\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_ctc\" title=\"js: ctc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">ctc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_getContractAddress\" class=\"pid\"></i>Returns a Promise for the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Address</span></span> of the connected Reach contract.<a href=\"#p_140\" details are omitted.<a href=\"#p_141\" class=\"pid\">141</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_ctc.getEventTys\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"ctc.getEventTys\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"ctc.getEventTys() => Record<string, ReachType[]>\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn83\" class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Promise</span></span> that results in the value of the API.\n  This function may throw an error if the API is not available.<a class=\"pid\">167</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_Event\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"Event\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"Event<T> : { when: Time, what: T }\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn101\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_Event\" title=\"js: Event\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">T</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> : { when</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> Time</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-punctuation)\">,</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> what</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">:</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">T</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> }</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_168\" class=\"pid\"></i>An <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_Event\" title=\"js: Event\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></a></span> is instantiated with it's corresponding type declared in Reach.<a href=\"#p_168\" class=\"pid\">168</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_169\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">next</span></span> will wait for the next <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></span> to occur, returning the time the event occurred\n  and the arguments to the event.<a href=\"#p_169\" class=\"pid\">169</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_170\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">nextUpToTime</span></span> is the same as <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">next</span></span>, except it will only return events up to the given time <code>t</code> (inclusive).\n  If time <code>t</code> has passed and no more events within the time frame are available, it will stop waiting and return <code>undefined</code>.<a href=\"#p_170\" class=\"pid\">170</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_171\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">seek</span></span> will set the internal time of the EventStream to the given argument.\n  The EventStream will use this time as the minimum bound when searching for <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></span>s.<a href=\"#p_171\" class=\"pid\">171</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_172\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">seekNow</span></span> will set the internal time of the EventStream to the latest network time.\n  The EventStream will use this time as the minimum bound when searching for <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></span>s.<a href=\"#p_172\" class=\"pid\">172</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_173\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">lastTime</span></span> will return the last network time that an <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></span> was emitted.<a href=\"#p_173\" class=\"pid\">173</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_174\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">monitor</span></span> accepts a function of type <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_Event\" title=\"js: Event\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">T</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">=&gt;</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\"> </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">void</span></span> as an argument. The provided function will be\n  called whenever the <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">Event</span></span> occurs.<a href=\"#p_174\" class=\"pid\">174</a>\n</p>\n<h1 <code>zorkmid</code> are created in this code snippet, and then launched using <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_stdlib.launchToken\" title=\"js: stdlib.launchToken\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.launchToken</span></a></span> by the <span class=\"snip\"><span class=\"pid\"></i>Possible options to provide in <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">opts</span></span> include:<a href=\"#p_179\" class=\"pid\">179</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_180\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">decimals</span></span> The number of digits to use after the decimal point when displaying the non-network token.\n    The default is the same as the network token.<a href=\"#p_180\" class=\"pid\">180</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_181\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">supply</span></span> The total number of atomic token units to create.\n    The default is the maximum possible on the network.<a href=\"#p_181\" class=\"pid\">181</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_182\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">url</span></span> A URL where more information about the non-network token can be retrieved.\n    The default is no url.<a href=\"#p_182\" class=\"pid\">182</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_183\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">metadataHash</span></span> A hash of some metadata that is relevant to your non-network token.\n    The default is no metadata hash.<a href=\"#p_183\" class=\"pid\">183</a>\n  </li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_184\" class=\"pid\"></i>Algorand-only options:<a href=\"#p_184\" class=\"pid\">184</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_185\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">clawback</span></span> Address that can clawback (steal) holdings of the token.\n    The default is no clawback address.<a href=\"#p_185\" class=\"pid\">185</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_186\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">freeze</span></span> Address that can freeze holdings of the token.\n    The default is no freeze address.<a href=\"#p_186\" class=\"pid\">186</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_187\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">defaultFrozen</span></span> A boolean that indicates whether token holdings are frozen by default.\n    The default is <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">false</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_187\" class=\"pid\">187</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_188\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">reserve</span></span> Address that should hold reserves of the token.\n    The default is no reserve address.<a href=\"#p_188\" class=\"pid\">188</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_189\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">manager</span></span> Address that can manage the configuration of the token and destroy it.\n    The default is no manager address.<a href=\"#p_189\" class=\"pid\">189</a>\n  </li>\n  <li>\n    <i id=\"p_190\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">note</span></span> A <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Uint8Array</span></span> for the <code>Note</code> field of the asset creation transaction.\n    The default is no note.<a href=\"#p_190\" class=\"pid\">190</a>\n  </li>\n</ul>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_191\" class=\"pid\"></i>For more information on Algorand-only options, see\n  <a href=\"https://developer.algorand.org/docs/get-details/transactions/transactions/#asset-parameters\" target=\"_blank\">https://developer.algorand.org/docs/get-details/transactions/transactions/#asset-parameters</a>.<a href=\"#p_191\" class=\"pid\">191</a>\n</p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js-network\" class=\"pid\"></i>Returns a Promise that will only be resolved after the specified consensus network time.\n  In isolated testing modes, this will also force time to pass on the network, usually by sending trivial transactions.\n  An <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_isolated%20testing%20mode\">isolated testing mode</span> is a <code>REACH_CONNECTOR_MODE</code> that matches\n  <code>$NET-devnet</code> for all valid <code>$NET</code>, or when <code>REACH_ISOLATED_NETWORK</code> is set.<a href=\"#p_198\" class=\"pid\">198</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_199\" connector, allows you to adjust the transaction parameters that Reach uses when it creates and signs transactions.<a href=\"#p_207\" class=\"pid\">207</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_208\" class=\"pid\"></i>It accepts a function that takes three arguments:<a href=\"#p_208\" class=\"pid\">208</a></p>\n<ol>\n  <li><i id=\"p_209\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>who</code>: a <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_T_Address\" title=\"js: T_Address\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">T_Address</span></a></span> value of the sender;<a href=\"#p_209\" class=\"pid\">209</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_210\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>sra</code>: an unstable and undocumented object that may help you identify the transaction being created;<a href=\"#p_210\" class=\"pid\">210</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_211\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>params</code>: the base Algorand transaction parameters.<a href=\"#p_211\" class=\"pid\">211</a></li>\n</ol>\n<p><i id=\"p_212\" class=\"pid\"></i>It must return a new Algorand transaction parameter object.<a href=\"#p_212\" class=\"pid\">212</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_213\" class=\"pid\"></i>This is mostly useful for using <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/appinit/#rsh_ALGO\" title=\"rsh: ALGO\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">ALGO</span></a><a href=\"/rsh/consensus/#rsh_ALGO.blockSeed\" title=\"rsh: ALGO.blockSeed\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.blockSeed</span></a></span>, so you can adjust the transaction validity, like in the example above.<a href=\"#p_213\" class=\"pid\">213</a></p>\n<h1 class=\"pid\"></i>This code converts the last 8 bytes of <code>b1</code>, <code>b2</code>, <code>b3</code> and <code>b4</code> to an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" class=\"pid\">243</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_244\" class=\"pid\"></i>If the string is less than 8 bytes long, this function will convert the entire string to an <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/compute/#rsh_UInt\" title=\"rsh: UInt\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">UInt</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_244\" class=\"pid\">244</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><i id=\"p_245\" unit with custom decimal place</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_246\" class=\"pid\"></i>These functions handle amounts in a network's standard unit and its atomic unit.\n  A <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_standard%20unit\">standard unit</span> is the network token unit most commonly associated with a network.\n  For example, the standard unit of Ethereum is ETH.\n  An <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_atomic%20unit\">atomic unit</span> is the smallest unit of measure for the standard unit.\n  For example, the atomic unit of Ethereum is WEI.\n  An atomic unit is <span class=\"term\" id=\"term_atomic\">atomic</span>, which means it cannot be divided into smaller units.<a href=\"#p_246\" class=\"pid\">246</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_247\" class=\"pid\"></i>Some consensus networks, typically those with proof-of-stake, have minimum balances on their accounts, so this is exposed as <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_minimumBalance\" title=\"js: minimumBalance\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">minimumBalance</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_247\" class=\"pid\">247</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_248\" class=\"pid\"></i>Because there are 1,000,000,000,000,000,000 WEI in 1 ETH,\n  BigNumber is used to represet values in WEI.<a href=\"#p_248\" class=\"pid\">248</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_249\" class=\"pid\"></i>Quantities of a network token should always be passed into Reach\n  in the token's atomic unit.<a href=\"#p_249\" class=\"pid\">249</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_250\" class=\"pid\"></i><span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_bigNumberify\" title=\"js: bigNumberify\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.bigNumberify</span></a></span> is transparently applied to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_formatCurrency\" title=\"js: formatCurrency\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.formatCurrency</span></a></span>'s and <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">stdlib</span><a href=\"/frontend/#js_formatWithDecimals\" title=\"js: formatWithDecimals\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.formatWithDecimals</span></a></span>'s first arguments.<a href=\"#p_250\" class=\"pid\">250</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_formatAddress\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"formatAddress\"></span><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_stdlib.formatAddress\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"stdlib.formatAddress\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"stdlib.formatAddress(acc: Account | Address) => string\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn141\" title=\"Copy to var(--shiki-color-text)\"> string</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_251\" class=\"pid\"></i>Formats the address in the way the user would expect to see it:<a href=\"#p_251\" class=\"pid\">251</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li><i id=\"p_252\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Ethereum, it is a hex-encoded string starting with <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-string-expression)\">'0x'</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_252\" class=\"pid\">252</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_253\" class=\"pid\"></i>On Algorand, it is a base32-encoded string, ending with the checksum.<a href=\"#p_253\" class=\"pid\">253</a></li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_254\" class=\"pid\"></i>Example:<a href=\"#p_254\" class=\"pid\">254</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div function\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">function</span></a></span> that takes in <code>addr</code> on line 32.\n  Line 33 formats <code>addr</code> based on the consensus network's encoding.\n  On line 35, the formatted <code>addr</code> (now stored as <code>address</code>) is revealed to the user in the console.<a href=\"#p_255\" class=\"pid\">255</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i also accepted from the frontend\n  in all places that Reach expects an address.<a href=\"#p_256\" class=\"pid\">256</a>\n</p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js-ask\" class=\"refHeader\">Reading User Input: href=\"#p_263\" class=\"pid\">263</a></p>\n<h1 id=\"ref-frontends-js-test\" class=\"refHeader\">Writing tests: <code>test</code><a aria-hidden=\"true\" tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#ref-frontends-js-test\"><span class=\"icon icon-link\"></span></a></h1>\n<p><i id=\"p_264\" class=\"pid\"></i>The Reach JavaScript standard library provides the <code>test</code> object for constructing automated tests.<a href=\"#p_264\" class=\"pid\">264</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_test\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"test\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet <i id=\"p_265\" class=\"pid\"></i>You do not need to use this module.\n  We think it is a great way to write tests, but it doesn't do anything you couldn't do on your own or with any other of the excellent JavaScript testing frameworks.<a href=\"#p_265\" class=\"pid\">265</a>\n</p>\n<hr>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_266\" class=\"pid\"></i>On initialization, <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test\" title=\"js: test\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">test</span></a></span> will read the process's command-line arguments and interpret them as a list of tests to run.\n  If no arguments are given, then all tests will be run.<a href=\"#p_266\" class=\"pid\">266</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_267\" class=\"pid\"></i>If you want to inspect this set of tests-to-run, then you can use the functions:<a href=\"#p_267\" class=\"pid\">267</a></p>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_test.shouldRun\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"test.shouldRun\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"test.shouldRun(x: string): named <code>id</code> that does not fail if <code>actual</code> is the same as <code>expected</code>.\n  Records additional information in the log from <code>xtra</code>.<a href=\"#p_271\" class=\"pid\"></i>Runs a check named <code>id</code> that expects <code>f</code> to throw an exception that satisfies the regex <code>expected</code>.<a href=\"#p_274\" class=\"pid\"></i>Schedules a test named <code>id</code> which is run by calling <code>f</code>.<a href=\"#p_275\" class=\"pid\">275</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_276\" class=\"pid\"></i>This uses <span var(--shiki-color-text)\">stdlib</span></span>) and a compiled backend (like given to <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_acc\" title=\"js: acc\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">acc</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_contract\" title=\"js: contract\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.contract</span></a></span>) and returns two objects:<a href=\"#p_277\" class=\"pid\">277</a></p>\n<ol>\n  <li><i id=\"p_278\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>exports</code> --- The object containing all of the <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/rsh/module/#rsh_export\" title=\"rsh: export\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">export</span></a></span>ed functions.<a href=\"#p_278\" class=\"pid\">278</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_279\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>chkExport</code> --- A function to run tests on a particular function.<a href=\"#p_279\" class=\"pid\">279</a></li>\n</ol>\n<p><i id=\"p_280\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>chkExport</code> takes two arguments:<a href=\"#p_280\" class=\"pid\">280</a></p>\n<ol>\n  <li><i id=\"p_281\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>fn</code> --- The name of a function to test<a href=\"#p_281\" class=\"pid\">281</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_282\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>go</code> --- A function that accepts a customized version of <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test\" title=\"js: test\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">test</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test.chk\" title=\"js: test.chk\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.chk</span></a></span> and <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test\" title=\"js: test\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">test</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test.chkErr\" title=\"js: test.chkErr\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.chkErr</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_282\" class=\"pid\">282</a></li>\n</ol>\n<p><i id=\"p_283\" class=\"pid\"></i>These customized versions are referred to as:<a href=\"#p_283\" class=\"pid\">283</a></p>\n<ol>\n  <li><i id=\"p_284\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>chkf</code> --- A function that accepts a domain and an expected range and ensures that the actual function result matches it.<a href=\"#p_284\" class=\"pid\">284</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_285\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>chkfErr</code> --- A function that accepts an expected exception value and a domain and ensures that the actual function throws the exception.<a href=\"#p_285\" class=\"pid\">285</a></li>\n</ol>\n<p><i id=\"p_286\" class=\"pid\"></i>This function uses <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test\" title=\"js: test\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">test</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test.one\" title=\"js: test.one\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.one</span></a></span> internally.<a href=\"#p_286\" class=\"pid\">286</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p><span class=\"ref\" id=\"js_test.run\" data-scope=\"js\" data-symbol=\"test.run\"></span></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet unnumbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"test.run(opts): Promise<void>\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn154\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test\" title=\"js: test\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">test</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test.run\" title=\"js: test.run\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">.run</span></a><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">(opts): </span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">Promise</span><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-keyword)\">&lt;void&gt;</span></li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_287\" class=\"pid\"></i>Runs any tests scheduled with <span class=\"snip\"><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test\" title=\"js: test\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">test</span></a><a href=\"/frontend/#js_test.one\" title=\"js: test.one\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">.one</span></a></span>.<a href=\"#p_287\" class=\"pid\">287</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_288\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>opts.howManyAtOnce</code> may be a number that determines how many tests to run in parallel.\n  It defaults to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">1</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_288\" class=\"pid\">288</a>\n</p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_289\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>opts.exitOnFail</code> may be a boolean that determines whether testing should end whenever the first test fails.\n  It defaults to <span class=\"snip\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-constant)\">true</span></span>.<a href=\"#p_289\" class=\"pid\">289</a>\n</p>\n<p><i id=\"p_290\" class=\"pid\"></i>When testing is finished, the process will be exited with an error code signifying whether any tests failed.<a href=\"#p_290\" class=\"pid\">290</a></p>\n<p><i id=\"p_291\" class=\"pid\"></i>In addition, three lines will be outputed with the following format:<a href=\"#p_291\" class=\"pid\">291</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"var RESULTS_B64='x'\nvar SUMMARY='y'\nvar STATUS='z'\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn155\" title=\"Copy to clipboard\"></a></div><ol class=\"snippet\"><li value=\"1\">var RESULTS_B64='x'</li><li value=\"2\">var SUMMARY='y'</li><li value=\"3\">var STATUS='z'</li></ol></pre>\n<p><i id=\"p_292\" class=\"pid\"></i>where<a href=\"#p_292\" class=\"pid\">292</a></p>\n<ul>\n  <li><i id=\"p_293\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>x</code> is the base64 encoding of test results in the JUnit format as accepted by tools like <a href=\"https://circleci.com/docs/2.0/collect-test-data/\" target=\"_blank\">CircleCI</a>.<a href=\"#p_293\" class=\"pid\">293</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_294\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>y</code> is a single line summary of how many tests failed<a href=\"#p_294\" class=\"pid\">294</a></li>\n  <li><i id=\"p_295\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>z</code> is a six character prefix suitable for using with <code>y</code>.<a href=\"#p_295\" class=\"pid\">295</a></li>\n</ul>\n<p><i id=\"p_296\" class=\"pid\"></i>A convenient way to consume this output is with the following shell code:<a href=\"#p_296\" class=\"pid\">296</a></p>\n<pre class=\"snippet numbered\"><div class=\"codeHeader\">&nbsp;<a class=\"far fa-copy copyBtn\" data-clipboard-text=\"set -o pipefail +e\necho Running...\n${REACH} run index --- &quot;$@&quot; | tee log\nEXIT=$?\nsed -i 's/\\r//g' log\nsed -n 's/^var //p' log > log.sh\nsource log.sh\necho &quot;${RESULTS_B64}&quot; | base64 -d - > test_results.xml\ncat > message.sh <<END\nSTATUS=&quot;${STATUS}&quot;\nSUMMARY=&quot;${SUMMARY}&quot;\nEND\ngrep -v '^var ' log\necho &quot;${STATUS} ${SUMMARY}&quot;\nexit &quot;${EXIT}&quot;\" href=\"#\" id=\"copyBtn156\" value=\"12\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-token-function)\">END</span></li><li value=\"13\"><span style=\"color: var(--shiki-color-text)\">grep </span><span style=\"color: messages from CircleCI to Slack for continuous integration.<a href=\"#p_297\" class=\"pid\">297</a></p>\n<p>\n  <i id=\"p_298\" class=\"pid\"></i><code>opts.noVarOutput</code> may be a boolean that
